### [1] [TerraLingua: Emergence and Analysis of Open-endedness in LLM Ecologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16910)
*Giuseppe Paolo,Jamieson Warner,Hormoz Shahrzad,Babak Hodjat,Risto Miikkulainen,Elliot Meyerson*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了TerraLingua，一个具有资源限制和生命周期约束的持久性多智能体生态系统，用于研究自主智能体的开放式动态演化，实验观察到合作规范、劳动分工、治理尝试和累积性文化过程的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主智能体在现实数字生态系统中的广泛应用，理解它们如何协调、形成制度并积累共享文化成为科学和实践的优先事项。现有的大语言模型模拟通常基于静态或无后果的环境，缺乏对真实世界约束的建模。

Method: 引入TerraLingua平台，这是一个持久性多智能体生态系统，对智能体施加资源约束和有限生命周期限制。智能体创造超越个体的持久性人工制品，塑造未来的互动和选择压力。采用AI人类学家系统分析智能体行为、群体结构和人工制品演化。

Result: 在实验条件下，观察到合作规范、劳动分工、治理尝试以及与累积性文化过程一致的分支化人工制品谱系的出现。不同实验运行的差异化结果可追溯到特定的创新和组织结构。

Conclusion: TerraLingua为刻画人工群体中累积性文化和社会组织的机制提供了平台，可作为指导现实世界智能体群体实现社会有益结果的基础。

Abstract: As autonomous agents increasingly operate in real-world digital ecosystems, understanding how they coordinate, form institutions, and accumulate shared culture becomes both a scientific and practical priority. This paper introduces TerraLingua, a persistent multi-agent ecology designed to study open-ended dynamics in such systems. Unlike prior large language model simulations with static or consequence-free environments, TerraLingua imposes resource constraints and limited lifespans for the agents. As a result, agents create artifacts that persist beyond individuals, shaping future interactions and selection pressures. To characterize the dynamics, an AI Anthropologist systematically analyzes agent behavior, group structure, and artifact evolution. Across experimental conditions, the results reveal the emergence of cooperative norms, division of labor, governance attempts, and branching artifact lineages consistent with cumulative cultural processes. Divergent outcomes across experimental runs can be traced back to specific innovations and organizational structures. TerraLingua thus provides a platform for characterizing the mechanisms of cumulative culture and social organization in artificial populations, and can serve as a foundation for guiding real-world agentic populations to socially beneficial outcomes.

</details>


### [2] [Impacts of Electric Vehicle Charging Regimes and Infrastructure Deployments on System Performance: An Agent-Based Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16961)
*Jiahua Hu,Hai L. Vu,Wynita Griggs,Hao Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文利用基于主体的建模框架评估充电基础设施部署策略，发现基于利用率的优化部署策略能降低系统总成本，且目的地充电与途中充电之间存在行为关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电动汽车的快速增长需要更有效的充电基础设施规划。基础设施布局不仅决定部署成本，还会重塑充电行为并影响整体系统性能。此外，目的地充电和途中充电代表不同的充电模式，具有不同的功率需求，可能导致截然不同的基础设施部署结果。

Method: 本研究应用基于主体的建模框架，基于墨尔本（澳大利亚）大都市区的综合表示，在三种充电模式下生成轨迹级的潜在公共充电需求。评估了两种部署策略：基于优化的方法和基于利用率细化的方法，并在不同的基础设施布局中进行比较。

Result: 结果显示，基于利用率细化的部署降低了系统总成本（包括基础设施部署成本和用户广义充电成本），在组合充电模式下改善最为显著。具体而言，更有效地分配交流慢速充电器重塑了目的地充电行为，进而减少了对途中充电的不必要依赖，并降低了与途中充电相关的绕行成本。

Conclusion: 目的地充电与途中充电模式之间的相互作用凸显了行为关联性，证明了在充电基础设施规划中考虑用户响应和多种充电模式的重要性。

Abstract: The rapid growth of electric vehicles (EVs) requires more effective charging infrastructure planning. Infrastructure layout not only determines deployment cost, but also reshapes charging behavior and influences overall system performance. In addition, destination charging and en-route charging represent distinct charging regimes associated with different power requirements, which may lead to substantially different infrastructure deployment outcomes. This study applies an agent-based modeling framework to generate trajectory-level latent public charging demand under three charging regimes based on a synthetic representation of the Melbourne (Australia) metropolitan area. Two deployment strategies, an optimization-based approach and a utilization-refined approach, are evaluated across different infrastructure layouts. Results show that utilization-refined deployments reduce total system cost, accounting for both infrastructure deployment cost and user generalized charging cost, with the most significant improvement observed under the combined charging regime. In particular, a more effective allocation of AC slow chargers reshapes destination charging behavior, which in turn reduces unnecessary reliance on en-route charging and lowers detour costs associated with en-route charging. This interaction highlights the behavioral linkage between destination and en-route charging regimes and demonstrates the importance of accounting for user response and multiple charging regimes in charging infrastructure planning.

</details>


### [3] [Ablation Study of a Fairness Auditing Agentic System for Bias Mitigation in Early-Onset Colorectal Cancer Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17179)
*Amalia Ionescu,Jose Guadalupe Hernandez,Jui-Hsuan Chang,Emily F. Wong,Paul Wang,Jason H. Moore,Tiffani J. Bright*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本研究评估了一种基于双智能体的AI系统在早发性结直肠癌（EO-CRC）模型公平性审计中的表现，发现结合检索增强生成（RAG）的智能体系统在识别差异方面取得了与专家参考陈述最高的语义相似度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能在临床环境中的广泛应用，有限的监督和领域专业知识可能导致算法偏见和安全风险持续存在。本研究旨在探索智能体AI系统是否能够支持生物医学机器学习模型的公平性审计，特别是针对存在人口统计学差异记录的早发性结直肠癌（EO-CRC）。

Method: 研究采用双智能体架构，包括一个综合EO-CRC差异文献的领域专家智能体和一个推荐敏感属性与公平性指标的公平性顾问智能体。研究通过消融实验比较了三种Ollama大语言模型（8B、20B和120B参数）在三种配置下的表现：仅预训练LLM、无RAG智能体和有RAG智能体。

Result: 实验结果显示，在所有测试模型中，结合RAG的智能体配置在语义相似度方面表现最佳，特别是在差异识别任务上，其生成的陈述与专家参考陈述最为接近，表明该系统可以有效支持临床AI的公平性审计。

Conclusion: 结合检索增强生成（RAG）的智能体AI系统有望帮助扩展临床AI模型的公平性审计规模，为解决算法偏见和安全风险提供一种可扩展的辅助方案。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly used in clinical settings, yet limited oversight and domain expertise can allow algorithmic bias and safety risks to persist. This study evaluates whether an agentic AI system can support auditing biomedical machine learning models for fairness in early-onset colorectal cancer (EO-CRC), a condition with documented demographic disparities. We implemented a two-agent architecture consisting of a Domain Expert Agent that synthesizes literature on EO-CRC disparities and a Fairness Consultant Agent that recommends sensitive attributes and fairness metrics for model evaluation. An ablation study compared three Ollama large language models (8B, 20B, and 120B parameters) across three configurations: pretrained LLM-only, Agent without Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), and Agent with RAG. Across models, the Agent with RAG achieved the highest semantic similarity to expert-derived reference statements, particularly for disparity identification, suggesting agentic systems with retrieval may help scale fairness auditing in clinical AI.

</details>


### [4] [Agentic Cognitive Profiling: Realigning Automated Alzheimer's Disease Detection with Clinical Construct Validity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17392)
*Jiawen Kang,Kun Li,Dongrui Han,Jinchao Li,Junan Li,Lingwei Meng,Xixin Wu,Helen Meng*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了代理认知分析框架（ACP），通过将标准化评估分解为原子认知任务并协调专业LLM代理提取可验证评分要素，在阿尔茨海默病筛查中实现了90.5%的任务评分匹配率和85.3%的预测准确率，证明了构建效度与预测性能无需权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化阿尔茨海默病（AD）筛查主要采用归纳式模式识别范式，直接将输入信号映射到结果标签，这种范式牺牲了临床方案的构建效度来换取统计捷径，导致模型缺乏可解释性。

Method: 提出代理认知分析框架（ACP），将标准化评估分解为原子认知任务，协调专业LLM代理提取可验证评分要素。核心设计是将语义理解与测量解耦，将所有量化工作委托给确定性函数调用，从而减轻幻觉问题并恢复构建效度。

Result: 在包含402名参与者、跨越多个认知域的八项结构化认知任务的临床标注语料库上，该框架实现了90.5%的任务评分匹配率和85.3%的AD预测准确率，超越了现有主流基线方法，同时能够生成基于行为证据的可解释认知档案。

Conclusion: 研究证明了构建效度和预测性能无需权衡，为开发能够提供解释而不仅仅是预测的AD筛查系统开辟了新路径，使自动化筛查重新与临床方案逻辑对齐。

Abstract: Automated Alzheimer's Disease (AD) screening has predominantly followed the inductive paradigm of pattern recognition, which directly maps the input signal to the outcome label. This paradigm sacrifices construct validity of clinical protocol for statistical shortcuts. This paper proposes Agentic Cognitive Profiling (ACP), an agentic framework that realigns automated screening with clinical protocol logic across multiple cognitive domains. Rather than learning opaque mappings from transcripts to labels, the framework decomposes standardized assessments into atomic cognitive tasks and orchestrates specialized LLM agents to extract verifiable scoring primitives. Central to our design is decoupling semantic understanding from measurement by delegating all quantification to deterministic function calling, thereby mitigating hallucination and restoring construct validity. Unlike popular datasets that typically comprise around a hundred participants under a single task, we evaluate on a clinically-annotated corpus of 402 participants across eight structured cognitive tasks spanning multiple cognitive domains. The framework achieves 90.5% score match rate in task examination and 85.3% accuracy in AD prediction, surpassing popular baselines while generating interpretable cognitive profiles grounded in behavioral evidence. This work demonstrates that construct validity and predictive performance need not be traded off, charting a path toward AD screening systems that explain rather than merely predict.

</details>


### [5] [In Trust We Survive: Emergent Trust Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17564)
*Qianpu Chen,Giulio Barbero,Mike Preuss,Derya Soydaner*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了Emergent Trust Learning (ETL)，一种轻量级、基于信任的控制算法，可嵌入现有AI智能体，使其在竞争性共享资源环境中达成合作。该方法仅依赖个体奖励和局部观察，计算和通信开销极小，在多种环境中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在竞争性游戏环境和共享资源场景中，传统AI智能体往往难以自发达成合作，容易陷入资源争夺和社会困境。现有方法可能需要全局信息、复杂通信或高昂计算成本。因此，本文旨在设计一种轻量级、可插拔的机制，使智能体在仅有个体奖励和局部观察的条件下，通过内部信任状态调节行为，实现合作并避免资源枯竭和被剥削。

Method: 提出Emergent Trust Learning (ETL)算法：每个智能体维护一个紧凑的内部信任状态，该状态动态调节记忆、探索和动作选择。ETL以即插即用方式集成到现有智能体中，仅依赖个体奖励和局部观察，无需全局信息，且带来极小的计算和通信开销。

Result: 在三种环境中进行评估：1) 网格资源世界中，信任智能体减少冲突、防止长期资源枯竭并保持竞争性个体回报；2) 具有强社会困境和随机楼层分配的层级塔环境中，ETL维持高生存率，并在长期强制贪婪阶段后恢复合作；3) 在重复囚徒困境中，算法泛化到策略元博弈，能与互惠对手保持合作，同时避免被背叛者长期剥削。

Conclusion: ETL为多智能体竞争环境中的合作问题提供了一种高效、轻量且通用的解决方案，证明了基于内部信任状态的简单机制足以在复杂社会困境中涌现合作行为，具有良好的泛化性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: We introduce Emergent Trust Learning (ETL), a lightweight, trust-based control algorithm that can be plugged into existing AI agents. It enables these to reach cooperation in competitive game environments under shared resources. Each agent maintains a compact internal trust state, which modulates memory, exploration, and action selection. ETL requires only individual rewards and local observations and incurs negligible computational and communication overhead.
  We evaluate ETL in three environments: In a grid-based resource world, trust-based agents reduce conflicts and prevent long-term resource depletion while achieving competitive individual returns. In a hierarchical Tower environment with strong social dilemmas and randomised floor assignments, ETL sustains high survival rates and recovers cooperation even after extended phases of enforced greed. In the Iterated Prisoner's Dilemma, the algorithm generalises to a strategic meta-game, maintaining cooperation with reciprocal opponents while avoiding long-term exploitation by defectors. Code will be released upon publication.

</details>

### [6] [KANtize: Exploring Low-bit Quantization of Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks for Efficient Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17230)
*Sohaib Errabii,Olivier Sentieys,Marcello Traiola*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本研究探索了低比特量化对KAN网络的影响，发现B样条可量化至2-3比特且精度损失可忽略，通过预计算查找表替代递归算法显著降低计算复杂度并提升硬件效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KAN网络相比MLP具有更好的参数效率和可解释性，但其样条函数的评估增加了推理时的计算复杂度。传统量化方法可降低计算复杂度，但低比特量化（低于8比特）对KAN网络的影响及其在减少计算复杂度方面的有效性尚未被探索。

Method: 研究低比特量化对KAN网络的影响，提出使用低比特量化预计算查找表替代递归B样条算法，以降低计算复杂度并提升硬件效率，同时保持精度。

Result: B样条可量化至2-3比特且精度损失可忽略；ResKAN18在无精度损失下实现50倍BitOps减少；8比特预计算查找表在GPU上实现最高2.9倍加速；在FPGA脉动阵列加速器上，3比特量化相比8比特减少36%资源使用、提高50%时钟频率并提升1.24倍加速；在28nm FD-SOI ASIC上，3比特相比16比特实现72%面积减少和50%最大频率提升。

Conclusion: 低比特量化对KAN网络有效，可显著降低计算复杂度并提升硬件效率，同时保持模型精度，为KAN网络的高效部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks (KANs) have gained attention for their potential to outperform Multi-Layer Perceptrons (MLPs) in terms of parameter efficiency and interpretability. Unlike traditional MLPs, KANs use learnable non-linear activation functions, typically spline functions, expressed as linear combinations of basis splines (B-splines). B-spline coefficients serve as the model's learnable parameters. However, evaluating these spline functions increases computational complexity during inference. Conventional quantization reduces this complexity by lowering the numerical precision of parameters and activations. However, the impact of quantization on KANs, and especially its effectiveness in reducing computational complexity, is largely unexplored, particularly for quantization levels below 8 bits. The study investigates the impact of low-bit quantization on KANs and its impact on computational complexity and hardware efficiency. Results show that B-splines can be quantized to 2-3 bits with negligible loss in accuracy, significantly reducing computational complexity. Hence, we investigate the potential of using low-bit quantized precomputed tables as a replacement for the recursive B-spline algorithm. This approach aims to further reduce the computational complexity of KANs and enhance hardware efficiency while maintaining accuracy. For example, ResKAN18 achieves a 50x reduction in BitOps without loss of accuracy using low-bit-quantized B-spline tables. Additionally, precomputed 8-bit lookup tables improve GPU inference speedup by up to 2.9x, while on FPGA-based systolic-array accelerators, reducing B-spline table precision from 8 to 3 bits cuts resource usage by 36%, increases clock frequency by 50%, and enhances speedup by 1.24x. On a 28nm FD-SOI ASIC, reducing the B-spline bit-width from 16 to 3 bits achieves 72% area reduction and 50% higher maximum frequency.

</details>


### [7] [ReLMXEL: Adaptive RL-Based Memory Controller with Explainable Energy and Latency Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17309)
*Panuganti Chirag Sai,Gandholi Sarat,R. Raghunatha Sarma,Venkata Kalyan Tavva,Naveen M*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了ReLMXEL框架，一个可解释的多智能体在线强化学习方法，用于动态优化内存控制器参数，显著降低了延迟和能耗，同时提高了决策透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代计算系统中，降低延迟和能耗对于提高内存系统效率至关重要。传统的内存控制器参数优化方法缺乏适应性和透明度，需要一种能够动态优化并解释其决策的新方法。

Method: 采用可解释的多智能体在线强化学习框架，利用奖励分解技术动态优化内存控制器参数。该方法在内存控制器内部运行，利用详细的内存行为指标来指导决策过程。

Result: 实验表明，ReLMXEL在各种工作负载上相比基线配置均取得了稳定的性能提升，并且能够根据特定工作负载的内存访问行为进行优化。通过在学习过程中引入可解释性，不仅提高了性能，还增加了控制决策的透明度。

Conclusion: ReLMXEL为更负责任和自适应的内存系统设计铺平了道路，证明了将可解释性融入内存控制器优化过程的可行性和价值。

Abstract: Reducing latency and energy consumption is critical to improving the efficiency of memory systems in modern computing. This work introduces ReLMXEL (Reinforcement Learning for Memory Controller with Explainable Energy and Latency Optimization), a explainable multi-agent online reinforcement learning framework that dynamically optimizes memory controller parameters using reward decomposition. ReLMXEL operates within the memory controller, leveraging detailed memory behavior metrics to guide decision-making. Experimental evaluations across diverse workloads demonstrate consistent performance gains over baseline configurations, with refinements driven by workload-specific memory access behaviour. By incorporating explainability into the learning process, ReLMXEL not only enhances performance but also increases the transparency of control decisions, paving the way for more accountable and adaptive memory system designs.

</details>


### [8] [Enabling RISC-V Vector Code Generation in MLIR through Custom xDSL Lowerings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17800)
*Jie Lei,Héctor Martínez,Adrián Castelló*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合MLIR和xDSL的编译方法，通过自定义中间表示和转换Pass，实现了从高级抽象到RISC-V向量扩展(RVV)内联函数的完整编译路径。实验表明，生成的GEMM微内核在真实RISC-V平台上相比OpenBLAS基线获得了最高12.2 GFLOPS（基线5.1 GFLOPS）的性能，性能提升达10-35%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着RISC-V在高性能和科学计算领域的广泛采用，对面向RISC-V向量扩展(RVV)的性能可移植代码需求日益增加。然而，现有编译器基础设施在从高级表示到低级实现生成优化的RVV代码方面提供的端到端支持有限，特别是现有的MLIR发行版缺乏将高级抽象映射到RVV内联函数的实用降低路径，限制了其在生产级RISC-V内核中的适用性。

Method: 本文提出了一种结合MLIR与xDSL的编译方法来填补RVV代码生成所需的缺失降低阶段。通过在xDSL中实现的自定义中间表示和转换Pass，系统地将高级操作转换为专门的、硬件感知的C代码，这些代码调用RVV内联函数。生成的内核被发射为可移植的C函数，可直接集成到现有应用中，无需修改周边软件栈即可实现增量采用。研究以通用矩阵乘法(GEMM)内核为案例进行了验证。

Result: 在两个真实RISC-V平台(K230和BananaPi F3)上评估了生成的微内核，并与OpenBLAS进行了对比。实验涵盖了方阵基准测试和基于BERT-Large模型的Transformer工作负载。所提出的方法持续优于OpenBLAS，性能达到12.2 GFLOPS，而基线仅为5.1 GFLOPS，在评估的工作负载中提供了10-35%的性能提升。

Conclusion: 实验结果证明，将MLIR与xDSL相结合为RISC-V平台提供了一条实用的、可移植的优化代码生成路径，有效解决了现有编译器基础设施在RVV代码生成方面的不足，为RISC-V平台的高性能计算应用提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: The growing adoption of RISC-V in high-performance and scientific computing has increased the need for performance-portable code targeting the RISC-V Vector (RVV) extension. However, current compiler infrastructures provide limited end-to-end support for generating optimized RVV code from high-level representations to low-level implementations. In particular, existing MLIR distributions lack practical lowering paths that map high-level abstractions to RVV intrinsics, limiting their applicability for production-ready RISC-V kernels. This paper presents a compilation approach that combines MLIR with xDSL to bridge the missing lowering stages required for RVV code generation. Using custom intermediate representations and transformation passes implemented in xDSL, we systematically translate high-level operations into specialized, hardware-aware C code invoking RVV intrinsics. The resulting kernels are emitted as portable C functions that can be directly integrated into existing applications, enabling incremental adoption without modifying surrounding software stacks. We demonstrate the approach on the General Matrix Multiplication (GEMM) kernel and evaluate the generated micro-kernels on two real RISC-V platforms, the K230 and the BananaPi F3, comparing against OpenBLAS for both square-matrix benchmarks and transformer-based workloads derived from the BERT-Large model. When integrated into a matrix multiplication kernel, the proposed approach consistently outperforms OpenBLAS, reaching up to 12.2 GFLOPS compared to the baseline's 5.1 GFLOPS and providing performance improvements between 10--35\% across the evaluated workloads. These results demonstrate that combining MLIR with xDSL provides a practical pathway to portable, optimized code generation for RISC-V platforms.

</details>

### [9] [Generative AI-assisted Participatory Modeling in Socio-Environmental Planning under Deep Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17021)
*Zhihao Pei,Nir Lipovetzky,Angela M. Rojas-Arevalo,Fjalar J. de Haan,Enayat A. Moallemi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种利用大型语言模型（LLM）辅助社会环境规划中问题概念化的模板化工作流程，通过ChatGPT在湖泊问题和电力市场问题上的演示，证明了LLM能有效促进参与式建模过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度不确定性下的社会环境规划中，问题概念化过程通常依赖参与式建模，需要将利益相关者的自然语言描述转化为定量模型，这一过程复杂且耗时，因此亟需一种方法来简化和加速该过程。

Method: 提出了一种模板化工作流程，利用大型语言模型（LLM）从利益相关者的直观问题描述中识别关键模型组件，探索问题的多元视角，将组件组装为统一模型，并通过迭代对话在Python中实现模型，同时结合人工验证与修正。

Result: 使用ChatGPT 5.2 Instant在湖泊问题和电力市场问题上演示了该工作流程。在两个案例中，经过少量迭代的人工验证和修正后，均获得了可接受的模型输出，表明LLM能有效辅助问题概念化。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型可作为促进社会环境规划中参与式建模问题概念化过程的有效工具，能够显著简化研究人员的建模工作流程。

Abstract: Socio-environmental planning under deep uncertainty requires researchers to identify and conceptualize problems before exploring policies and deploying plans. In practice and model-based planning approaches, this problem conceptualization process often relies on participatory modeling to translate stakeholders' natural-language descriptions into a quantitative model, making this process complex and time-consuming. To facilitate this process, we propose a templated workflow that uses large language models for an initial conceptualization process. During the workflow, researchers can use large language models to identify the essential model components from stakeholders' intuitive problem descriptions, explore their diverse perspectives approaching the problem, assemble these components into a unified model, and eventually implement the model in Python through iterative communication. These results will facilitate the subsequent socio-environmental planning under deep uncertainty steps. Using ChatGPT 5.2 Instant, we demonstrated this workflow on the lake problem and an electricity market problem, both of which demonstrate socio-environmental planning problems. In both cases, acceptable outputs were obtained after a few iterations with human verification and refinement. These experiments indicated that large language models can serve as an effective tool for facilitating participatory modeling in the problem conceptualization process in socio-environmental planning.

### [10] [Transformers are Bayesian Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17063)
*Gregory Coppola*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文从理论和实验两个角度证明了Transformer本质上是一个贝叶斯网络，其层级结构严格对应信念传播算法，并指出幻觉问题源于缺乏有限概念空间的grounding。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer是当前AI领域的主导架构，但其工作机制仍未被充分理解。本文旨在为Transformer为何有效提供一个精确的理论解释，将其与经典的贝叶斯网络理论建立严格联系。

Method: 通过五个方面建立理论框架：1)证明任意sigmoid transformer等价于在隐式因子图上执行加权循环信念传播；2)构造性证明transformer可在任意知识库上实现精确信念传播；3)证明能产生精确后验的sigmoid transformer必为BP权重的唯一性；4)解析transformer层的布尔结构，注意力为AND、前馈网络为OR，严格交替构成Pearl的gather/update算法；5)通过实验验证所有理论结果。

Result: 证明了transformer与贝叶斯网络的等价性，获得了形式化验证；实验证实了理论预测；进一步证明可验证的推断需要有限概念空间，幻觉是缺乏概念grounding的结构性后果，不能通过规模化解决。

Conclusion: Transformer本质上是一个贝叶斯网络，其推理机制可通过信念传播理论精确解释。幻觉问题并非可通过规模化修复的bug，而是缺乏有限概念空间grounding的结构性必然结果。这一发现为理解Transformer的工作原理和局限性提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Transformers are the dominant architecture in AI, yet why they work remains poorly understood. This paper offers a precise answer: a transformer is a Bayesian network. We establish this in five ways.
  First, we prove that every sigmoid transformer with any weights implements weighted loopy belief propagation on its implicit factor graph. One layer is one round of BP. This holds for any weights -- trained, random, or constructed. Formally verified against standard mathematical axioms.
  Second, we give a constructive proof that a transformer can implement exact belief propagation on any declared knowledge base. On knowledge bases without circular dependencies this yields provably correct probability estimates at every node. Formally verified against standard mathematical axioms.
  Third, we prove uniqueness: a sigmoid transformer that produces exact posteriors necessarily has BP weights. There is no other path through the sigmoid architecture to exact posteriors. Formally verified against standard mathematical axioms.
  Fourth, we delineate the AND/OR boolean structure of the transformer layer: attention is AND, the FFN is OR, and their strict alternation is Pearl's gather/update algorithm exactly.
  Fifth, we confirm all formal results experimentally, corroborating the Bayesian network characterization in practice. We also establish the practical viability of loopy belief propagation despite the current lack of a theoretical convergence guarantee.
  We further prove that verifiable inference requires a finite concept space. Any finite verification procedure can distinguish at most finitely many concepts. Without grounding, correctness is not defined. Hallucination is not a bug that scaling can fix. It is the structural consequence of operating without concepts. Formally verified against standard mathematical axioms.

</details>


### [11] [Cascade-Aware Multi-Agent Routing: Spatio-Temporal Sidecars and Geometry-Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17112)
*Davide Di Gioia*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轻量级的在线几何控制方法，通过自适应选择欧氏或双曲风险模型来估计执行图中的路由风险，从而解决现有调度器对拓扑几何结构不敏感的问题。在Genesis 3基准测试中，该方法将整体胜率从基线的50.4%提升至87.2%，在树状结构场景中提升高达48-68个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI推理系统的符号图网络调度器仅优化负载和适配度，却忽视了对失败传播至关重要的拓扑几何特性：树状结构中的单一失败可能指数级级联，而稠密环状图中的失败往往自我受限。这种“几何盲点”导致了系统级性能损失，亟需一种能够感知并适应不同拓扑几何的路由风险估计方法。

Method: 作者提出了一种在线几何控制框架，包含三个核心组件：（i）欧氏时空传播基线模型；（ii）带时间衰减（及可选突发激励）的双曲路由风险模型；（iii）基于结构特征的几何选择器。该选择器是一个紧凑的MLP（9->12->1），使用六个拓扑统计量和三个几何感知信号（BFS壳增长斜率、环秩范数、拟合庞加莱曲率）来动态选择最优几何模型。

Result: 在Genesis 3基准分布上，自适应几何切换将最难的非树状结构的胜率从固定双曲变体的64-72%提升至92%，整体胜率达87.2%。相比无时空旁路的原生bandit/LinUCB基线（整体50.4%，树状结构仅20%），完整旁路系统实现了+36.8pp的整体提升，在树状结构中提升+48至+68pp，仅用133个参数即显著缓解了几何盲点的失败传播问题。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过引入仅133个参数的轻量级几何感知旁路，可以显著改善高级AI推理系统中的失败传播控制。该方法成功填补了调度器的可观测性缺口，证明了拓扑几何感知对于执行图路由优化的关键价值，为高能力执行图系统的鲁棒性提升提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: A common architectural pattern in advanced AI reasoning systems is the symbolic graph network: specialized agents or modules connected by delegation edges, routing tasks through a dynamic execution graph. Current schedulers optimize load and fitness but are geometry-blind: they do not model how failures propagate differently in tree-like versus cyclic regimes. In tree-like delegation, a single failure can cascade exponentially; in dense cyclic graphs, failures tend to self-limit. We identify this observability gap, quantify its system-level cost, and propose a lightweight mitigation.
  We formulate online geometry control for route-risk estimation on time-indexed execution graphs with route-local failure history. Our approach combines (i) a Euclidean spatio-temporal propagation baseline, (ii) a hyperbolic route-risk model with temporal decay (and optional burst excitation), and (iii) a learned geometry selector over structural features. The selector is a compact MLP (9->12->1) using six topology statistics plus three geometry-aware signals: BFS shell-growth slope, cycle-rank norm, and fitted Poincare curvature. On the Genesis 3 benchmark distribution, adaptive switching improves win rate in the hardest non_tree regime from 64-72% (fixed hyperbolic variants) to 92%, and achieves 87.2% overall win rate.
  To measure total system value, we compare against Genesis 3 routing without any spatio-temporal sidecar, using only native bandit/LinUCB signals (team fitness and mean node load). This baseline achieves 50.4% win rate overall and 20% in tree-like regimes; the full sidecar recovers 87.2% overall (+36.8 pp), with +48 to +68 pp gains in tree-like settings, consistent with a cascade-sensitivity analysis. Overall, a 133-parameter sidecar substantially mitigates geometry-blind failure propagation in one high-capability execution-graph system.

</details>


### [12] [How Clued up are LLMs? Evaluating Multi-Step Deductive Reasoning in a Text-Based Game Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17169)
*Rebecca Ansell,Autumn Toney-Wails*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文构建了基于文本的多智能体“妙探寻凶”游戏作为多步演绎推理测试平台。实验发现LLM智能体在完整游戏过程中难以维持一致的演绎推理，微调未能可靠提升性能，有时甚至增加了推理量却未提高推理精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估大语言模型智能体的多步演绎推理能力具有挑战性。经典桌游“妙探寻凶”需要玩家通过逐步收集线索进行逻辑排除和推理，是测试多步演绎推理的理想场景，且现有研究对该能力的系统性评估不足。

Method: 实现基于文本的多智能体版经典桌游“妙探寻凶”作为规则型测试平台；选用GPT-4o-mini和Gemini-2.5-Flash两种模型构建六个智能体；通过18场模拟游戏评估多步演绎推理能力；探究在结构化逻辑谜题上微调是否能迁移改善游戏推理表现。

Result: 在18场模拟游戏中，智能体仅取得4次正确胜利；微调未能可靠改善性能，部分情况下反而增加推理量却未提升推理精度。

Conclusion: 当前LLM智能体在需要多步演绎推理的复杂任务中表现不佳，存在难以维持一致推理链的问题；简单地在结构化逻辑谜题上微调并不能有效迁移到游戏推理场景。

Abstract: Deducing whodunit proves challenging for LLM agents. In this paper, we implement a text-based multi-agent version of the classic board game Clue as a rule-based testbed for evaluating multi-step deductive reasoning, with six agents drawn from GPT-4o-mini and Gemini-2.5-Flash. We further investigate whether fine-tuning on structured logic puzzles transfers to improved in-game reasoning and gameplay. Across 18 simulated games, agents achieve only four correct wins, indicating difficulty in maintaining consistent deductive reasoning over the course of a full game. Additionally, we find that fine-tuning does not reliably improve performance and, in some cases, appears to increase reasoning volume without improving reasoning precision.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体系统缺乏训练方法的指导原则，且当前LLM生成的想法往往看似合理但实际无效。为了训练能够从实践中学习的智能体，需要一种自动生成高质量ML任务的方法。

Method: 提出了一种新型合成环境生成流程，自动生成与SWE-agent框架兼容的机器学习挑战，包括主题采样、数据集提议和代码生成。生成的任务基于真实ML数据集（通过Huggingface API验证），并通过自调试循环提高质量。采用教师-学生训练范式，从GPT-5采样轨迹，用于训练Qwen3-4B和Qwen3-8B模型。

Conclusion: 该合成环境生成流程为训练能够从实践中学习的ML智能体提供了有效的方法，验证了合成任务在提升模型研究能力方面的价值。

Abstract: With the advent of AI agents, automatic scientific discovery has become a tenable goal. To make progress on training agents that can learn from doing, we provide a novel synthetic environment generation pipeline targeting machine learning agents. Our pipeline automatically synthesizes machine learning challenges compatible with the SWE-agent framework, covering topic sampling, dataset proposal, and code generation. The resulting synthetic tasks are 1) grounded in real machine learning datasets, because the proposed datasets are verified against the Huggingface API and are 2) verified for higher quality with a self-debugging loop. To validate the effectiveness of our synthetic tasks, we tackle MLGym, a benchmark for machine learning tasks. From the synthetic tasks, we sample trajectories from a teacher model (GPT-5), then use the trajectories to train a student model (Qwen3-4B and Qwen3-8B). The student models trained with our synthetic tasks achieve improved performance on MLGym, raising the AUP metric by 9% for Qwen3-4B and 12% for Qwen3-8B.

### [14] [Draft-and-Prune: Improving the Reliability of Auto-formalization for Logical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17233)
*Zhiyu Ni,Zheng Liang,Liangcheng Song,Chenrui Cao,Xian Zhang,Alberto Sangiovanni-Vincentelli,Pierluigi Nuzzo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Draft-and-Prune (D&P)框架，通过多样化和验证机制增强自动形式化(AF)的逻辑推理能力，在多个基准测试上显著提升性能，部分达到满分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动形式化(AF)流程存在脆弱性问题：程序可能执行失败或编码错误语义。虽然先前工作通过基于求解器反馈的修复缓解了语法失败，但减少语义失败仍是主要瓶颈。

Method: 提出Draft-and-Prune (D&P)推理时框架：1) 起草多个自然语言计划并基于此生成程序；2) 剪枝可执行但矛盾或歧义的形式化结果；3) 对幸存路径通过多数投票聚合预测。

Result: 在四个基准测试(AR-LSAT、ProofWriter、PrOntoQA、LogicalDeduction)上显著提升AF推理性能。AR-LSAT上GPT-4达78.43%，GPT-4o达78.00%，显著优于MAD-LOGIC和CLOVER基线。PrOntoQA和LogicalDeduction达到100%准确率。

Conclusion: D&P框架在不增加额外监督的情况下，有效增强了基于AF的逻辑推理能力，证明了多样化和验证策略对提升自动形式化质量的有效性。

Abstract: Auto-formalization (AF) translates natural-language reasoning problems into solver-executable programs, enabling symbolic solvers to perform sound logical deduction. In practice, however, AF pipelines are currently brittle: programs may fail to execute, or execute but encode incorrect semantics. While prior work largely mitigates syntactic failures via repairs based on solver feedback, reducing semantics failures remains a major bottleneck. We propose Draft-and-Prune (D&P), an inference-time framework that improves AF-based logical reasoning via diversity and verification. D&P first drafts multiple natural-language plans and conditions program generation on them. It further prunes executable but contradictory or ambiguous formalizations, and aggregates predictions from surviving paths via majority voting. Across four representative benchmarks (AR-LSAT, ProofWriter, PrOntoQA, LogicalDeduction), D&P substantially strengthens AF-based reasoning without extra supervision. On AR-LSAT, in the AF-only setting, D&P achieves 78.43% accuracy with GPT-4 and 78.00% accuracy with GPT-4o, significantly outperforming the strongest AF baselines MAD-LOGIC and CLOVER. D&P then attains near-ceiling performance on the other benchmarks, including 100% on PrOntoQA and LogicalDeduction.

</details>


### [15] [Governed Memory: A Production Architecture for Multi-Agent Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17787)
*Hamed Taheri*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文针对企业AI中多智能体节点缺乏共享记忆与统一治理的问题，提出了Governed Memory（受治理的记忆）这一共享记忆与治理层，通过双记忆模型、分层治理路由、反射界检索与闭环模式生命周期四大机制，在实验中实现了高事实召回率与治理合规性、零跨实体泄露、显著Token削减，且不损害检索质量，已在Personize.ai投产。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业AI在工作流中部署了大量自治智能体节点，这些节点对同一实体进行操作却缺乏共享记忆与统一治理。这种记忆治理缺口导致了五个结构性挑战：跨智能体工作流的记忆孤岛；跨团队与工具的治理碎片化；非结构化记忆无法被下游系统使用；自治多步执行中的冗余上下文交付；以及缺乏反馈循环导致的隐性质量退化。

Method: 提出Governed Memory共享记忆与治理层，包含四个机制：1）双记忆模型，结合开放集原子事实与模式强制的类型化属性；2）分层治理路由，实现渐进式上下文交付；3）反射界检索，具备实体作用域隔离；4）闭环模式生命周期，支持AI辅助创作与自动化逐属性细化。通过受控实验验证各机制有效性，并在LoCoMo基准上评估整体检索质量。

Result: 在受控实验（N=250，五种内容类型）中：事实召回率达99.6%（双模态互补覆盖）；治理路由精度92%；渐进式上下文交付减少50%的Token消耗；在500次对抗性查询中实现零跨实体泄露；对抗性治理合规率100%；输出质量在每实体约七个受治理记忆时趋于饱和。在LoCoMo基准上整体准确率为74.8%，验证了治理与模式强制不损害检索质量。系统已在Personize.ai生产环境部署。

Conclusion: Governed Memory有效解决了企业AI中的记忆治理缺口，在确保安全隔离与合规治理的前提下实现了高效检索与上下文优化，证明了治理机制可系统化嵌入而不牺牲性能，为企业级多智能体系统提供了可落地的治理框架。

Abstract: Enterprise AI deploys dozens of autonomous agent nodes across workflows, each acting on the same entities with no shared memory and no common governance. We identify five structural challenges arising from this memory governance gap: memory silos across agent workflows; governance fragmentation across teams and tools; unstructured memories unusable by downstream systems; redundant context delivery in autonomous multi-step executions; and silent quality degradation without feedback loops. We present Governed Memory, a shared memory and governance layer addressing this gap through four mechanisms: a dual memory model combining open-set atomic facts with schema-enforced typed properties; tiered governance routing with progressive context delivery; reflection-bounded retrieval with entity-scoped isolation; and a closed-loop schema lifecycle with AI-assisted authoring and automated per-property refinement. We validate each mechanism through controlled experiments (N=250, five content types): 99.6% fact recall with complementary dual-modality coverage; 92% governance routing precision; 50% token reduction from progressive delivery; zero cross-entity leakage across 500 adversarial queries; 100% adversarial governance compliance; and output quality saturation at approximately seven governed memories per entity. On the LoCoMo benchmark, the architecture achieves 74.8% overall accuracy, confirming that governance and schema enforcement impose no retrieval quality penalty. The system is in production at Personize.ai.

</details>


### [16] [Graph-Native Cognitive Memory for AI Agents: Formal Belief Revision Semantics for Versioned Memory Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17244)
*Young Bin Park*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Kumiho，一种基于AGM信念修正理论的形式化图原生认知记忆架构，在LoCoMo-Plus基准上达到93.3%准确率，大幅超越现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI智能体记忆系统的独立组件虽有研究，但其架构整合与形式化理论基础仍待探索。本文旨在构建一个统一的形式化认知记忆架构，同时支持记忆管理与工作资产的版本化管理。

Method: 提出图原生认知记忆架构Kumiho，建立AGM信念修正框架与属性图记忆系统操作语义之间的对应关系，证明满足基本AGM公设和Hansson信念基公设。采用双存储模型（Redis工作记忆+Neo4j长期图），实现混合全文和向量检索，引入三项架构创新：前瞻索引、事件提取和客户端LLM重排序。

Result: 在LoCoMo基准上获得0.565的总体F1分数（n=1,986），包括97.5%的对抗性拒绝准确率；在LoCoMo-Plus基准上达到93.3%的法官准确率（n=401），独立复现结果为中80%范围，显著优于所有已发表基线（最佳Gemini 2.5 Pro仅45.7%）。模型无关性强，从GPT-4o-mini切换到GPT-4o可提升准确率且无需修改流程。

Conclusion: Kumiho成功实现了信念修正理论与图记忆系统的形式化统一，为AI智能体提供了可验证的认知记忆能力，在认知记忆基准上取得了实质性突破，证明了形式化理论基础对记忆架构设计的重要性。

Abstract: While individual components for AI agent memory exist in prior systems, their architectural synthesis and formal grounding remain underexplored. We present Kumiho, a graph-native cognitive memory architecture grounded in formal belief revision semantics. The structural primitives required for cognitive memory -- immutable revisions, mutable tag pointers, typed dependency edges, URI-based addressing -- are identical to those required for managing agent-produced work as versionable assets, enabling a unified graph-native architecture that serves both purposes. The central formal contribution is a correspondence between the AGM belief revision framework and the operational semantics of a property graph memory system, proving satisfaction of the basic AGM postulates (K*2--K*6) and Hansson's belief base postulates (Relevance, Core-Retainment). The architecture implements a dual-store model (Redis working memory, Neo4j long-term graph) with hybrid fulltext and vector retrieval. On LoCoMo (token-level F1), Kumiho achieves 0.565 overall F1 (n=1,986) including 97.5% adversarial refusal accuracy. On LoCoMo-Plus, a Level-2 cognitive memory benchmark testing implicit constraint recall, Kumiho achieves 93.3% judge accuracy (n=401); independent reproduction by the benchmark authors yielded results in the mid-80% range, still substantially outperforming all published baselines (best: Gemini 2.5 Pro, 45.7%). Three architectural innovations drive the results: prospective indexing (LLM-generated future-scenario implications indexed at write time), event extraction (structured causal events preserved in summaries), and client-side LLM reranking. The architecture is model-decoupled: switching the answer model from GPT-4o-mini (~88%) to GPT-4o (93.3%) improves end-to-end accuracy without pipeline changes, at a total evaluation cost of ~$14 for 401 entries.

### [17] [Contrastive Reasoning Alignment: Reinforcement Learning from Hidden Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17305)
*Haozheng Luo,Yimin Wang,Jiahao Yu,Binghui Wang,Yan Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CRAFT框架，通过优化隐藏状态空间中的目标，使大推理模型生成安全感知的推理轨迹，从而显著提升对越狱攻击的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御方法主要在输出层面操作，难以有效应对针对大推理模型的越狱攻击。作者旨在利用模型的推理能力和隐藏表示，在推理层面实现更深层次的安全对齐。

Method: CRAFT将对比表征学习与强化学习相结合，在隐藏状态空间中显式优化目标，分离安全与不安全的推理轨迹。理论证明，将潜在-文本一致性纳入GRPO可排除表面对齐策略，使其不成为局部最优解。

Result: 在Qwen3-4B-Thinking和R1-Distill-Llama-8B两个强推理模型及多个安全基准上的实验表明，CRAFT持续优于IPO和SafeKey等最先进防御方法。与基线模型相比，推理安全性平均提升79.0%，最终响应安全性提升87.7%。

Conclusion: 隐藏空间推理对齐是提升大模型安全性的有效途径，CRAFT框架通过在潜在空间构建支持鲁棒安全对齐的几何结构，实现了对越狱攻击的有效防御。

Abstract: We propose CRAFT, a red-teaming alignment framework that leverages model reasoning capabilities and hidden representations to improve robustness against jailbreak attacks. Unlike prior defenses that operate primarily at the output level, CRAFT aligns large reasoning models to generate safety-aware reasoning traces by explicitly optimizing objectives defined over the hidden state space. Methodologically, CRAFT integrates contrastive representation learning with reinforcement learning to separate safe and unsafe reasoning trajectories, yielding a latent-space geometry that supports robust, reasoning-level safety alignment. Theoretically, we show that incorporating latent-textual consistency into GRPO eliminates superficially aligned policies by ruling them out as local optima. Empirically, we evaluate CRAFT on multiple safety benchmarks using two strong reasoning models, Qwen3-4B-Thinking and R1-Distill-Llama-8B, where it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art defenses such as IPO and SafeKey. Notably, CRAFT delivers an average 79.0% improvement in reasoning safety and 87.7% improvement in final-response safety over the base models, demonstrating the effectiveness of hidden-space reasoning alignment.

### [18] [InfoDensity: Rewarding Information-Dense Traces for Efficient Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17310)
*Chengwei Wei,Jung-jae Kim,Longyin Zhang,Shengkai Chen,Nancy F. Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出InfoDensity奖励框架，通过结合AUC奖励和单调性奖励来优化LLM推理过程，在保持或提升准确率的同时显著减少token使用，实现准确率与效率的良好平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法仅优化最终响应长度而忽略中间推理步骤的质量，导致模型易受奖励黑客攻击。作者认为冗长性不是单纯的长度问题，而是中间推理质量差的症状，需要从推理步骤的信息密度角度解决。

Method: 1. 通过跟踪推理步骤间答案分布的条件熵进行实证研究，发现高质量推理轨迹具有两个特性：低不确定性收敛和单调进展；2. 提出InfoDensity奖励框架，结合AUC奖励和单调性奖励作为推理质量的统一度量，并通过长度缩放项加权以鼓励更简洁地实现相同质量。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试上，InfoDensity在准确率方面匹配或超越最先进基线，同时显著减少token使用量，实现了准确率与效率之间的强平衡。

Conclusion: 高质量推理轨迹具有信息密度高的特征（每一步相对于总推理长度都贡献有意义的熵减少），InfoDensity框架通过奖励信息密集的推理过程，有效解决了LLM推理中的冗长性问题，证明了从中间推理质量角度优化的重要性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) with extended reasoning capabilities often generate verbose and redundant reasoning traces, incurring unnecessary computational cost. While existing reinforcement learning approaches address this by optimizing final response length, they neglect the quality of intermediate reasoning steps, leaving models vulnerable to reward hacking. We argue that verbosity is not merely a length problem, but a symptom of poor intermediate reasoning quality. To investigate this, we conduct an empirical study tracking the conditional entropy of the answer distribution across reasoning steps. We find that high-quality reasoning traces exhibit two consistent properties: low uncertainty convergence and monotonic progress. These findings suggest that high-quality reasoning traces are informationally dense, that is, each step contributes meaningful entropy reduction relative to the total reasoning length. Motivated by this, we propose InfoDensity, a reward framework for RL training that combines an AUC-based reward and a monotonicity reward as a unified measure of reasoning quality, weighted by a length scaling term that favors achieving equivalent quality more concisely. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that InfoDensity matches or surpasses state-of-the-art baselines in accuracy while significantly reducing token usage, achieving a strong accuracy-efficiency trade-off.

### [19] [Physics-informed offline reinforcement learning eliminates catastrophic fuel waste in maritime routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17319)
*Aniruddha Bora,Julie Chalfant,Chryssostomos Chryssostomidis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PIER是一个离线强化学习框架，用于国际航运的节能风险感知路径规划。在墨西哥湾七条航线一年的AIS数据验证中，相比大圆航线平均减少10%的CO2排放，并将极端燃油消耗（>1.5倍中位数）的发生率从4.8%降至0.5%，燃油消耗方差降低3.5倍，且不受预报不确定性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 国际航运贡献约3%的全球温室气体排放，然而当前航线路径规划仍主要依赖启发式方法，缺乏基于物理模型和实际数据的优化策略。现有方法在面对预报不确定性时性能下降显著，且无法有效避免极端燃油消耗事件。因此，需要一种不依赖在线模拟器、能够融合物理约束和历史数据的智能路径规划方法。

Method: 提出PIER（Physics-Informed, Energy-efficient, Risk-aware routing）离线强化学习框架，包括三个核心组件：（1）基于物理信息的状态构建，融合历史船舶追踪数据和海洋再分析产品；（2）示范增强的离线数据收集策略；（3）解耦的事后安全屏障机制。该框架无需在线模拟器，仅依赖局部观测即可做出决策，不依赖天气预报信息。

Result: 在2023年全年墨西哥湾七条航线的AIS数据验证中（每方法840个回合），PIER相比大圆航线平均减少10%的CO2排放；极端燃油消耗事件从4.8%降至0.5%（减少9倍）；单次航行燃油方差降低3.5倍（p<0.001），均值节约的Bootstrap 95%置信区间为[2.9%, 15.7%]；与实际AIS船舶行为部分验证显示与最快真实过境一致，方差低23.1倍；在预报不确定性下，A*路径优化的波浪防护性能下降4.5倍，而PIER保持恒定性能。

Conclusion: PIER成功实现了无需预报信息的节能安全航运路径规划，显著降低了燃油消耗及其波动性，有效消除了灾难性燃油浪费事件。该框架结合物理约束、离线强化学习和安全屏障的设计架构具有良好的泛化能力，可推广应用于野火疏散、飞机轨迹优化和未知地形自主导航等领域。

Abstract: International shipping produces approximately 3% of global greenhouse gas emissions, yet voyage routing remains dominated by heuristic methods. We present PIER (Physics-Informed, Energy-efficient, Risk-aware routing), an offline reinforcement learning framework that learns fuel-efficient, safety-aware routing policies from physics-calibrated environments grounded in historical vessel tracking data and ocean reanalysis products, requiring no online simulator. Validated on one full year (2023) of AIS data across seven Gulf of Mexico routes (840 episodes per method), PIER reduces mean CO2 emissions by 10% relative to great-circle routing. However, PIER's primary contribution is eliminating catastrophic fuel waste: great-circle routing incurs extreme fuel consumption (>1.5x median) in 4.8% of voyages; PIER reduces this to 0.5%, a 9-fold reduction. Per-voyage fuel variance is 3.5x lower (p<0.001), with bootstrap 95% CI for mean savings [2.9%, 15.7%]. Partial validation against observed AIS vessel behavior confirms consistency with the fastest real transits while exhibiting 23.1x lower variance. Crucially, PIER is forecast-independent: unlike A* path optimization whose wave protection degrades 4.5x under realistic forecast uncertainty, PIER maintains constant performance using only local observations. The framework combines physics-informed state construction, demonstration-augmented offline data, and a decoupled post-hoc safety shield, an architecture that transfers to wildfire evacuation, aircraft trajectory optimization, and autonomous navigation in unmapped terrain.

To address these systemic misalignments, we introduce RideJudge, a Progressive Visual-Logic-Aligned Framework. Instead of relying on generic pre-training, we bridge the semantic gap via SynTraj, a synthesis engine that grounds abstract liability concepts into concrete trajectory patterns. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发现大型推理模型通过链式思维(CoT)获得卓越推理性能的同时，安全能力显著下降，但进一步观察发现这种安全退化仅在启用CoT时发生，禁用CoT时并未观察到此现象，这促使作者考虑鼓励LRMs在CoT生成前进行安全决策。

Method: 首先利用基于BERT的分类器从安全模型（如禁用CoT的LRM）中提取安全决策信号，然后将这些信号作为辅助监督整合到LRMs的安全对齐过程中，使安全梯度能够反向传播到LRMs的潜在表示，从而增强模型在CoT生成前的安全决策能力。

Result: 大量实验表明，所提方法在显著提升LRMs安全能力的同时，有效保持了模型的通用推理性能。通过将安全梯度反向传播到LRMs的潜在表示，成功增强了模型在CoT生成过程中的安全决策能力。

Conclusion: 研究证明了在CoT生成前进行安全决策的有效性，为解决LRMs安全能力退化问题提供了新的解决思路，实现了安全性与推理能力的良好平衡。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) achieved remarkable performance via chain-of-thought (CoT), but recent studies showed that such enhanced reasoning capabilities are at the expense of significantly degraded safety capabilities. In this paper, we reveal that LRMs' safety degradation occurs only after CoT is enabled, and this degradation is not observed when CoT is disabled. This observation motivates us to consider encouraging LRMs to make safety decisions before CoT generation. To this end, we propose a novel safety alignment method that promotes the safety decision-making of LRMs before starting CoT generation. Specifically, we first utilize a Bert-based classifier to extract safety decision signals from a safe model (e.g., a CoT-disabled LRM) and then integrate these signals into LRMs' safety alignment as auxiliary supervision. In this way, the safety gradients can be backpropagated to the LRMs' latent representations, effectively strengthening the LRMs' safety decision-making abilities against CoT generation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method substantially improves the safety capabilities of LRMs while effectively maintaining LRMs' general reasoning performance.

### [23] [From Digital Twins to World Models:Opportunities, Challenges, and Applications for Mobile Edge General Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17420)

Method: 首先阐明数字孪生与世界模型的概念差异，强调从基于物理、集中式、系统中心的模型向数据驱动、去中心化、以智能体为中心的内部模型转变；然后综述世界模型的设计原则、架构和核心组件，包括感知、潜在状态表示、动力学学习、基于想象的规划和记忆机制；最后探讨世界模型与数字孪生在无线边缘智能系统中的融合。

Abstract: The rapid evolution toward 6G and beyond communication systems is accelerating the convergence of digital twins and world models at the network edge. Traditional digital twins provide high-fidelity representations of physical systems and support monitoring, analysis, and offline optimization. However, in highly dynamic edge environments, they face limitations in autonomy, adaptability, and scalability. This paper presents a systematic survey of the transition from digital twins to world models and discusses its role in enabling edge general intelligence (EGI). First, the paper clarifies the conceptual differences between digital twins and world models and highlights the shift from physics-based, centralized, and system-centric replicas to data-driven, decentralized, and agent-centric internal models. This discussion helps readers gain a clear understanding of how this transition enables more adaptive, autonomous, and resource-efficient intelligence at the network edge. The paper reviews the design principles, architectures, and key components of world models, including perception, latent state representation, dynamics learning, imagination-based planning, and memory. In addition, it examines the integration of world models and digital twins in wireless EGI systems and surveys emerging applications in integrated sensing and communications, semantic communication, air-ground networks, and low-altitude wireless networks. Finally, this survey provides a systematic roadmap and practical insights for designing world-model-driven edge intelligence systems in wireless and edge computing environments. It also outlines key research challenges and future directions toward scalable, reliable, and interoperable world models for edge-native agentic AI.

### [24] [Proactive Knowledge Inquiry in Doctor-Patient Dialogue: Stateful Extraction, Belief Updating, and Path-Aware Action Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17425)
*Zhenhai Pan,Yan Liu,Jia You*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出将医患对话建模为部分可观测环境下的主动知识探查问题。框架结合了有状态提取、序贯信念更新、缺口感知状态建模、医疗知识混合检索以及POMDP-lite行动规划器，将文档记录视为持续探查循环的结构化投影，而非单一目标产物。

Abstract: Most automated electronic medical record (EMR) pipelines remain output-oriented: they transcribe, extract, and summarize after the consultation, but they do not explicitly model what is already known, what is still missing, which uncertainty matters most, or what question or recommendation should come next. We formulate doctor-patient dialogue as a proactive knowledge-inquiry problem under partial observability. The proposed framework combines stateful extraction, sequential belief updating, gap-aware state modeling, hybrid retrieval over objectified medical knowledge, and a POMDP-lite action planner. Instead of treating the EMR as the only target artifact, the framework treats documentation as the structured projection of an ongoing inquiry loop. To make the formulation concrete, we report a controlled pilot evaluation on ten standardized multi-turn dialogues together with a 300-query retrieval benchmark aggregated across dialogues. On this pilot protocol, the full framework reaches 83.3% coverage, 80.0% risk recall, 81.4% structural completeness, and lower redundancy than the chunk-only and template-heavy interactive baselines. These pilot results do not establish clinical generalization; rather, they suggest that proactive inquiry may be methodologically interesting under tightly controlled conditions and can be viewed as a conceptually appealing formulation worth further investigation for dialogue-based EMR generation. This work should be read as a pilot concept demonstration under a controlled simulated setting rather than as evidence of clinical deployment readiness. No implication of clinical deployment readiness, clinical safety, or real-world clinical utility should be inferred from this pilot protocol.

### [25] [When Only the Final Text Survives: Implicit Execution Tracing for Multi-Agent Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17445)
*Yi Nian,Haosen Cao,Shenzhe Zhu,Henry Peng Zou,Qingqing Luan,Yue Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了IET框架，通过在生成过程中嵌入密钥信号，实现了在无需执行日志的情况下对多智能体系统的词元级归属追踪和交互拓扑重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当多智能体系统产生错误或有害输出时，若执行日志和智能体标识符不可用，难以确定责任归属；现有的结构化交互过程（如委托和迭代细化）常被最终输出掩盖，缺乏对底层交互拓扑和智能体贡献的可追溯性。

Method: 提出IET（隐式执行追踪）框架，这是一种不依赖元数据的方法。在生成阶段，将智能体特定的密钥信号嵌入到词元分布中，使文本转化为自描述的执行追踪；在检测阶段，使用过渡感知评分方法识别智能体切换点并重构交互图。

Result: 实验表明，IET能够高精度地恢复智能体片段和协调结构，同时保持生成质量，实现了对多智能体语言系统的隐私保护审计。

Conclusion: IET为多智能体语言系统提供了一种有效的问责机制，可在保护隐私的前提下实现高质量的责任归属追踪。

Abstract: When a multi-agent system produces an incorrect or harmful answer, who is accountable if execution logs and agent identifiers are unavailable? Multi-agent language systems increasingly rely on structured interactions such as delegation and iterative refinement, yet the final output often obscures the underlying interaction topology and agent contributions. We introduce IET (Implicit Execution Tracing), a metadata-independent framework that enables token-level attribution directly from generated text and a simple mechanism for interaction topology reconstruction. During generation, agent-specific keyed signals are embedded into the token distribution, transforming the text into a self-describing execution trace detectable only with a secret key. At detection time, a transition-aware scoring method identifies agent handover points and reconstructs the interaction graph. Experiments show that IET recovers agent segments and coordination structure with high accuracy while preserving generation quality, enabling privacy-preserving auditing for multi-agent language systems.

### [26] [Informative Semi-Factuals for XAI: The Elaborated Explanations that People Prefer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17534)
*Saugat Aryal,Mark T. Keane*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了信息性半事实（ISF）方法，通过揭示隐藏特征来增强半事实解释的可解释性，解决了现有方法无法解释极端值变化不改变预测结果原因的问题，实验和用户研究证明了解释质量和用户偏好的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的半事实解释方法虽然能够找到不改变预测结果的单特征最大值变化（如“即使申请双倍贷款，你仍会被批准”），但无法解释为什么这些极端值变化不会改变结果，缺乏更深层次的因果信息。这种“黑盒式”的半事实解释限制了用户对AI决策系统的理解和信任。

Method: 提出了信息性半事实（ISF）算法，该算法在生成半事实解释的同时，识别并补充影响自动决策的隐藏特征信息。例如，不仅告诉用户“即使申请双倍贷款仍会被批准”，还会解释“正是你的良好信用评分使你能够借到双倍金额”。该方法结合了半事实生成与特征重要性分析，提供更详尽的解释。

Result: 在基准数据集上的实验结果表明，ISF方法在关键指标上生成了既具有信息性又高质量的半事实解释。用户研究进一步显示，相比于现有方法生成的简单半事实解释，人们更偏好这些详尽的解释，证明了方法的有效性和实用价值。

Conclusion: 信息性半事实方法成功弥合了半事实解释与因果推理之间的差距，通过揭示隐藏特征的影响机制，显著提升了XAI系统的透明度和用户理解度。该方法为构建更可信、更有用的AI解释系统提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Recently, in eXplainable AI (XAI), $\textit{even if}$ explanations -- so-called semi-factuals -- have emerged as a popular strategy that explains how a predicted outcome $\textit{can remain the same}$ even when certain input-features are altered. For example, in the commonly-used banking app scenario, a semi-factual explanation could inform customers about better options, other alternatives for their successful application, by saying "$\textit{Even if}$ you asked for double the loan amount, you would still be accepted". Most semi-factuals XAI algorithms focus on finding maximal value-changes to a single key-feature that do $\textit{not}$ alter the outcome (unlike counterfactual explanations that often find minimal value-changes to several features that alter the outcome). However, no current semi-factual method explains $\textit{why}$ these extreme value-changes do not alter outcomes; for example, a more informative semi-factual could tell the customer that it is their good credit score that allows them to borrow double their requested loan. In this work, we advance a new algorithm -- the $\textit{informative semi-factuals}$ (ISF) method -- that generates more elaborated explanations supplementing semi-factuals with information about additional $\textit{hidden features}$ that influence an automated decision. Experimental results on benchmark datasets show that this ISF method computes semi-factuals that are both informative and of high-quality on key metrics. Furthermore, a user study shows that people prefer these elaborated explanations over the simpler semi-factual explanations generated by current methods.

### [27] [Per-Domain Generalizing Policies: On Learning Efficient and Robust Q-Value Functions (Extended Version with Technical Appendix)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17544)
*Nicola J. Müller,Moritz Oster,Isabel Valera,Jörg Hoffmann,Timo P. Gros*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出学习Q值函数而非状态值函数来获取跨领域泛化策略，通过正则化项区分教师规划器采取和未采取的动作，在10个领域上性能优于状态值策略且与LAMA-first相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的状态值函数方法需要对每个后继状态进行处理，评估代价高昂。而Q值函数仅需处理当前状态，评估成本大幅降低。然而，普通的监督学习方法在训练Q值时表现不佳，因为它无法区分教师规划器采取的动作和未采取的动作。

Method: 提出学习Q值函数（Q-value functions）而非状态值函数，使用图神经网络表示。针对普通监督学习无法区分教师采取与未采取动作的问题，引入正则化项来强制这种区分，确保学习到的Q值能够正确反映动作的相对价值。

Result: Q值策略在10个测试领域中一致优于状态值策略，并与先进规划器LAMA-first具有竞争力。实验表明，通过正则化区分动作的方法有效解决了传统监督学习无法区分动作的问题，显著提升了策略性能。

Conclusion: 学习Q值函数是跨领域泛化策略学习的有效方法，相比传统的状态值函数方法具有更高的评估效率和更优的性能。正则化技术的引入对于确保Q值函数正确区分不同动作至关重要。

Abstract: Learning per-domain generalizing policies is a key challenge in learning for planning. Standard approaches learn state-value functions represented as graph neural networks using supervised learning on optimal plans generated by a teacher planner. In this work, we advocate for learning Q-value functions instead. Such policies are drastically cheaper to evaluate for a given state, as they need to process only the current state rather than every successor. Surprisingly, vanilla supervised learning of Q-values performs poorly as it does not learn to distinguish between the actions taken and those not taken by the teacher. We address this by using regularization terms that enforce this distinction, resulting in Q-value policies that consistently outperform state-value policies across a range of 10 domains and are competitive with the planner LAMA-first.

</details>


### [28] [VeriGrey: Greybox Agent Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17639)
*Yuntong Zhang,Sungmin Kang,Ruijie Meng,Marcel Böhme,Abhik Roychoudhury*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了VeriGrey，一种针对LLM智能体的灰盒测试方法，通过将工具调用序列作为反馈函数驱动测试过程，并结合提示词变异技术，有效发现了间接提示注入漏洞和恶意技能变体，在AgentDojo基准上比黑盒方法提高了33%的漏洞发现效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着代理式AI的快速发展，LLM智能体通过调用外部工具实现自主决策，但其与外部环境的自主交互引入了关键的安全风险。现有方法在发现不常见但危险的工具调用和潜在漏洞方面存在不足，需要一种能够有效探索智能体多样化行为并揭示安全风险的测试方法。

Method: 提出VeriGrey灰盒测试方法：1) 将工具调用序列作为反馈函数驱动测试过程，以发现导致异常行为的不常见工具调用；2) 设计变异算子对提示词进行变异，生成恶意注入提示；3) 通过将智能体任务与注入任务关联，使注入任务成为完成智能体功能的必要步骤；4) 结合模糊测试技术进行动态测试。

Result: 在AgentDojo基准测试中，使用GPT-4.1后端的VeriGrey比黑盒基线方法在发现间接提示注入漏洞方面效率提高33%。在真实案例研究中：1) 发现了Gemini CLI编码代理和OpenClaw个人助手的多种攻击场景；2) 在OpenClaw中，从10个恶意技能中发现恶意技能变体，在Kimi-K2.5后端成功率为100%(10/10)，在Opus 4.6后端成功率为90%(9/10)。

Conclusion: VeriGrey证明了动态灰盒测试方法在测试LLM智能体安全方面的价值，能够有效发现黑盒方法无法识别的安全漏洞。该方法为建立智能体保障框架奠定了基础，对提升代理式AI系统的安全性具有重要意义。

Abstract: Agentic AI has been a topic of great interest recently. A Large Language Model (LLM) agent involves one or more LLMs in the back-end. In the front end, it conducts autonomous decision-making by combining the LLM outputs with results obtained by invoking several external tools. The autonomous interactions with the external environment introduce critical security risks.
  In this paper, we present a grey-box approach to explore diverse behaviors and uncover security risks in LLM agents. Our approach VeriGrey uses the sequence of tools invoked as a feedback function to drive the testing process. This helps uncover infrequent but dangerous tool invocations that cause unexpected agent behavior. As mutation operators in the testing process, we mutate prompts to design pernicious injection prompts. This is carefully accomplished by linking the task of the agent to an injection task, so that the injection task becomes a necessary step of completing the agent functionality. Comparing our approach with a black-box baseline on the well-known AgentDojo benchmark, VeriGrey achieves 33% additional efficacy in finding indirect prompt injection vulnerabilities with a GPT-4.1 back-end.
  We also conduct real-world case studies with the widely used coding agent Gemini CLI, and the well-known OpenClaw personal assistant. VeriGrey finds prompts inducing several attack scenarios that could not be identified by black-box approaches. In OpenClaw, by constructing a conversation agent which employs mutational fuzz testing as needed, VeriGrey is able to discover malicious skill variants from 10 malicious skills (with 10/10= 100% success rate on the Kimi-K2.5 LLM backend, and 9/10= 90% success rate on Opus 4.6 LLM backend). This demonstrates the value of a dynamic approach like VeriGrey to test agents, and to eventually lead to an agent assurance framework.

### [29] [Sensi: Learn One Thing at a Time -- Curriculum-Based Test-Time Learning for LLM Game Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17683)
*Mohsen Arjmandi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Sensi是一种面向ARC-AGI-3游戏挑战的LLM智能体架构，通过双人架构、课程学习和可编程上下文窗口实现结构化的测试时学习。Sensi v2相比现有系统实现了50-94倍的样本效率提升（仅需约32次尝试），但研究揭示了新的瓶颈已从学习效率转移至感知落地问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在未知环境中部署时必须在测试时学习任务结构，但现有方法需要数千次交互才能形成有用的假设，效率极低。本研究旨在解决LLM智能体在测试时学习效率低下这一关键问题。

Method: Sensi架构通过三个核心机制实现结构化测试时学习：（1）将感知与行动分离的双人架构；（2）由外部状态机管理的课程学习系统；（3）使智能体上下文窗口可编程控制的数据库控制平面。此外还引入了LLM-as-judge组件，配合动态生成的评估标准来判断智能体何时已充分学习某一主题从而进入下一阶段。

Result: 实验结果显示：Sensi v1仅使用双人架构解决了2个游戏关卡；Sensi v2加入课程学习后虽未解决任何关卡，但仅用约32次行动尝试就完成了整个学习课程，相比需要1600-3000次尝试的可比系统实现了50-94倍的样本效率提升。研究精确诊断出失败模式为源自感知层的自我一致幻觉级联。

Conclusion: 该研究得出结论：架构瓶颈已从学习效率转移到感知落地问题，这是一个更易于处理的问题。通过精确诊断失败模式为自我一致幻觉级联，研究明确了后续改进方向，即需要重点解决感知层的落地问题而非学习效率问题。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents deployed in unknown environments must learn task structure at test time, but current approaches require thousands of interactions to form useful hypotheses. We present Sensi, an LLM agent architecture for the ARC-AGI-3 game-playing challenge that introduces structured test-time learning through three mechanisms: (1) a two-player architecture separating perception from action, (2) a curriculum-based learning system managed by an external state machine, and (3) a database-as-control-plane that makes the agents context window programmatically steerable. We further introduce an LLM-as-judge component with dynamically generated evaluation rubrics to determine when the agent has learned enough about one topic to advance to the next. We report results across two iterations: Sensi v1 solves 2 game levels using the two-player architecture alone, while Sensi v2 adds curriculum learning and solves 0 levels - but completes its entire learning curriculum in approximately 32 action attempts, achieving 50-94x greater sample efficiency than comparable systems that require 1600-3000 attempts. We precisely diagnose the failure mode as a self-consistent hallucination cascade originating in the perception layer, demonstrating that the architectural bottleneck has shifted from learning efficiency to perceptual grounding - a more tractable problem.

Central to our approach is a preference learning paradigm in which LLMs are economically aligned via post-training on extensive, heterogeneous transaction records across diverse product categories. This methodology enables the models to internalize and transfer latent consumer preference patterns, thereby mitigating the data sparsity issues prevalent in individual categories. To enhance simulation stability, we implement a mean-field mechanism designed to model the dynamic interactions between the product environment and customer populations, effectively stabilizing sampling processes within high-dimensional decision spaces. Furthermore, we propose a multi-agent discussion framework wherein specialized agents collaboratively process extensive product information. This architecture distributes cognitive load to alleviate single-agent attention bottlenecks and captures critical decision factors through structured dialogue. Experiments demonstrate that our framework achieves significant improvements in product selection accuracy, purchase quantity prediction, and simulation stability compared to existing economic and financial LLM simulation baselines. Our results substantiate the potential of large language models as a foundational pillar for high-fidelity, scalable decision simulation and latter analysis in the real economy based on foundational database.

Motivation: 自动驾驶技术在真实世界部署中面临数据稀缺、安全要求严格以及跨多样化环境泛化能力不足等关键瓶颈，亟需利用合成数据和虚拟环境来提供可扩展、可控且标注丰富的训练与评估场景。

Method: 从三个核心维度组织研究内容：(i) 合成数据在感知和规划中的应用；(ii) 基于数字孪生的系统验证仿真；(iii) 连接合成数据与真实世界数据的域适应策略。同时分析了视觉-语言模型和仿真真实感在增强场景理解和泛化能力中的作用，并提供了数据集、工具和仿真平台的详细分类法。

Result: 提供了数据集、工具和仿真平台的详细分类体系，分析了基准设计趋势，阐明了视觉-语言模型和仿真真实感在提升场景理解与泛化方面的作用，总结了当前技术发展现状。

Conclusion: 指出了Sim2Real迁移、可扩展安全验证、协同自动驾驶和仿真驱动的策略学习等关键挑战与开放研究方向，这些问题的解决将加速实现安全、可泛化且可全球部署的自动驾驶系统。

Abstract: Autonomous driving technologies have achieved significant advances in recent years, yet their real-world deployment remains constrained by data scarcity, safety requirements, and the need for generalization across diverse environments. In response, synthetic data and virtual environments have emerged as powerful enablers, offering scalable, controllable, and richly annotated scenarios for training and evaluation. This survey presents a comprehensive review of recent developments at the intersection of autonomous driving, simulation technologies, and synthetic datasets. We organize the landscape across three core dimensions: (i) the use of synthetic data for perception and planning, (ii) digital twin-based simulation for system validation, and (iii) domain adaptation strategies bridging synthetic and real-world data. We also highlight the role of vision-language models and simulation realism in enhancing scene understanding and generalization. A detailed taxonomy of datasets, tools, and simulation platforms is provided, alongside an analysis of trends in benchmark design. Finally, we discuss critical challenges and open research directions, including Sim2Real transfer, scalable safety validation, cooperative autonomy, and simulation-driven policy learning, that must be addressed to accelerate the path toward safe, generalizable, and globally deployable autonomous driving systems.

</details>


### [32] [Facts as First Class Objects: Knowledge Objects for Persistent LLM Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17781)
*Oliver Zahn,Simran Chana*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对比了大型语言模型的上下文记忆与知识对象（KOs）两种知识存储策略，发现KOs在准确率、成本和多跳推理上显著优于上下文记忆，并揭示了上下文记忆在生产环境中的容量限制、压缩损失和目标漂移等关键失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型正日益成为持久化知识工作者，而上下文记忆（将事实存储在提示中）作为默认策略被广泛采用。然而，其在生产环境中的可靠性尚未得到系统验证，亟需基准评估其性能边界并与替代方案进行比较。

Method: 研究设计了系统性基准测试，对比上下文记忆与知识对象（KOs）的性能。实验在Claude Sonnet 4.5等四个前沿模型上评估准确率、容量限制、成本效益和多跳推理能力。研究构建生产级部署场景，识别压缩损失和目标漂移等失败模式，并测试嵌入检索和神经记忆（Titans）在对抗性条件下的表现，最终提出密度自适应检索机制。

Result: Claude Sonnet 4.5在上下文窗口内从10到7,000个事实实现100%精确匹配准确率，但在生产部署中出现三重失败：容量限制（8,000事实时提示溢出）、压缩损失（摘要摧毁60%事实）、目标漂移（级联压缩侵蚀54%项目约束）。KOs在所有条件下达到100%准确率且成本降低252倍。多跳推理中，KOs达78.9%准确率，显著优于上下文记忆的31.6%。跨四个前沿模型的复现实验证实压缩损失是架构性问题。嵌入检索在对抗性事实上失败（精确率20%），神经记忆（Titans）能存储但无法按需检索。

Conclusion: 上下文记忆在生产部署中存在结构性缺陷，不适合作为持久化知识工作者的可靠记忆机制。KOs作为一种离散哈希寻址的记忆架构，提供了更可靠、高效且经济的替代方案。研究引入密度自适应检索机制并发布基准测试套件，为未来LLM记忆系统设计提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly serve as persistent knowledge workers, with in-context memory - facts stored in the prompt - as the default strategy. We benchmark in-context memory against Knowledge Objects (KOs), discrete hash-addressed tuples with O(1) retrieval. Within the context window, Claude Sonnet 4.5 achieves 100% exact-match accuracy from 10 to 7,000 facts (97.5% of its 200K window). However, production deployment reveals three failure modes: capacity limits (prompts overflow at 8,000 facts), compaction loss (summarization destroys 60% of facts), and goal drift (cascading compaction erodes 54% of project constraints while the model continues with full confidence). KOs achieve 100% accuracy across all conditions at 252x lower cost. On multi-hop reasoning, KOs reach 78.9% versus 31.6% for in-context. Cross-model replication across four frontier models confirms compaction loss is architectural, not model-specific. We additionally show that embedding retrieval fails on adversarial facts (20% precision at 1) and that neural memory (Titans) stores facts but fails to retrieve them on demand. We introduce density-adaptive retrieval as a switching mechanism and release the benchmark suite.

</details>


### [33] [RPMS: Enhancing LLM-Based Embodied Planning through Rule-Augmented Memory Synergy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17831)
*Zhenhang Yuan,Shenghai Yuan,Lihua Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出RPMS架构，通过规则检索、信念状态过滤和规则优先仲裁解决LLM智能体在封闭环境中的动作可行性与状态漂移问题，在ALFWorld上相比基线提升23.9pp（8B模型）和11.9pp（Claude），并在ScienceWorld上验证了方法的跨环境泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在封闭具身环境中常因动作需满足严格前置条件（如位置、库存、容器状态）且失败反馈稀疏而表现不佳。研究识别出两个结构耦合的失败模式：无效动作生成(P1)和状态漂移(P2)，二者相互放大形成恶性循环。

Method: 提出RPMS冲突管理架构：1) 通过结构化规则检索强制动作可行性；2) 通过轻量级信念状态约束记忆适用性；3) 通过规则优先仲裁解决规则与记忆间的冲突。

Result: ALFWorld（134个未见任务）：Llama 3.1 8B达到59.7%成功率（+23.9pp），Claude Sonnet 4.5达98.5%（+11.9pp）；8B增益中规则检索单独贡献+14.9pp（统计显著），是主导因素。场景记忆在经当前状态过滤和显式动作规则约束后从有害转为有益。ScienceWorld（GPT-4）平均分54.0 vs ReAct基线44.9。

Conclusion: 核心发现：情景记忆的条件性价值——未经接地时有损性能，但经当前状态过滤和显式规则约束后成为稳定正向因素。RPMS在结构迥异环境中均有效，验证了核心机制的跨环境泛化能力。

Abstract: LLM agents often fail in closed-world embodied environments because actions must satisfy strict preconditions -- such as location, inventory, and container states -- and failure feedback is sparse. We identify two structurally coupled failure modes: (P1) invalid action generation and (P2) state drift, each amplifying the other in a degenerative cycle. We present RPMS, a conflict-managed architecture that enforces action feasibility via structured rule retrieval, gates memory applicability via a lightweight belief state, and resolves conflicts between the two sources via rules-first arbitration. On ALFWorld (134 unseen tasks), RPMS achieves 59.7% single-trial success with Llama 3.1 8B (+23.9 pp over baseline) and 98.5% with Claude Sonnet 4.5 (+11.9 pp); of the 8B gain, rule retrieval alone contributes +14.9 pp (statistically significant), making it the dominant factor. A key finding is that episodic memory is conditionally useful: it harms performance on some task types when used without grounding, but becomes a stable net positive once filtered by current state and constrained by explicit action rules. Adapting RPMS to ScienceWorld with GPT-4 yields consistent gains across all ablation conditions (avg. score 54.0 vs. 44.9 for the ReAct baseline), providing transfer evidence that the core mechanisms hold across structurally distinct environments.

</details>


### [34] [AgentFactory: A Self-Evolving Framework Through Executable Subagent Accumulation and Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18000)
*Zhang Zhang,Shuqi Lu,Hongjin Qian,Di He,Zheng Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了AgentFactory，一种LLM智能体自我进化新范式，通过将成功的任务解决方案保存为可执行的Python子智能体代码（而非文本经验），实现能力的持续积累和复用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体自我进化方法主要将成功经验记录为文本提示或反思，在复杂场景下无法可靠保证高效的任务重复执行，且缺乏系统性的能力积累机制。

Method: 提出AgentFactory框架，将成功任务解决方案保存为标准化文档的可执行Python子智能体代码，基于执行反馈持续优化这些子智能体，使其随任务增多而变得更加鲁棒和高效。

Result: AgentFactory实现了能力的持续积累，可执行子智能体库随时间增长和改进，逐步减少类似任务所需的工作量，且代码形式支持跨Python环境的可移植性。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种可扩展的智能体能力积累方案，通过代码化保存和迭代优化实现了无需人工干预的持续自我进化，并已开源实现。

Abstract: Building LLM-based agents has become increasingly important. Recent works on LLM-based agent self-evolution primarily record successful experiences as textual prompts or reflections, which cannot reliably guarantee efficient task re-execution in complex scenarios. We propose AgentFactory, a new self-evolution paradigm that preserves successful task solutions as executable subagent code rather than textual experience. Crucially, these subagents are continuously refined based on execution feedback, becoming increasingly robust and efficient as more tasks are encountered. Saved subagents are pure Python code with standardized documentation, enabling portability across any Python-capable system. We demonstrate that AgentFactory enables continuous capability accumulation: its library of executable subagents grows and improves over time, progressively reducing the effort required for similar tasks without manual intervention. Our implementation is open-sourced at https://github.com/zzatpku/AgentFactory, and our demonstration video is available at https://youtu.be/iKSsuAXJHW0.

</details>

The ideas crystallized over fifteen years of research, conversation, and engineering practice -- beginning with a 2014 Stanford EE380 lecture on the physics of time in computing, sharpened through a 2016 email exchange with Leslie Lamport following a Papers We Love presentation of his seminal 1978 paper, and matured through the development of Open Atomic Ethernet (OAE). This document traces the concept development from its origins in the physics of entanglement and background-free time, through the recognition that Lamport's "happened-before" relation embeds a category mistake, to the practical engineering consequences documented in "Why iCloud Fails" and "What Distributed Computing Got Wrong." ### [36] [The 1/W Law: An Analytical Study of Context-Length Routing Topology and GPU Generation Gains for LLM Inference Energy Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17280)
*Huamin Chen,Xunzhuo Liu,Yuhan Liu,Junchen Jiang,Bowei He,Xue Liu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 在相同硬件上，不同上下文窗口大小的能效差异可达40倍；通过优化路由拓扑比升级硬件能更有效提升能效，结合两者可获得4.25倍的能效提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示GPU推理集群中上下文窗口大小对能效（tokens/W）的巨大影响，挑战传统认为升级硬件是提升能效主要手段的观点。

Method: 基于公开的H100功耗测量数据，使用校准的逻辑功耗模型和roofline吞吐量模型，通过inference-fleet-sim框架进行解析推导，未进行新的硬件实验。

Result: 推导出1/W定律：上下文窗口每翻倍，每瓦token数减半。在64K上下文时H100的tok/W为1.5（16个序列），4K时为17.6（256个序列）。双池上下文长度路由（FleetOpt）比同构集群提升约2.5倍能效；从H100升级到B200提升约1.7倍；两者结合可达4.25倍。MoE模型因激活权重而非总参数决定解码时间，能效优势明显。

Conclusion: 路由拓扑是比购买新硬件更强大的能效杠杆。优化服务上下文窗口的路由策略应成为提升推理能效的首要考虑因素。

Abstract: How many tokens can a GPU inference cluster deliver per watt? Across deployments of identical hardware, the answer varies by 40x -- not because of software inefficiency, but because of the serving context window. We derive the 1/W law: tokens per watt halves every time the context window doubles. A larger context window shrinks the KV-cache concurrency limit while leaving GPU power draw roughly unchanged. At 64K context, an H100 holds 16 sequences in flight (tok/W = 1.5); at 4K context, the same H100 holds 256 sequences (tok/W = 17.6).
  Routing topology -- which determines the effective context window each GPU services -- is a more powerful energy lever than buying newer hardware. Working from published H100 power measurements, a calibrated logistic power model, and a roofline throughput model, we derive these results analytically using the inference-fleet-sim framework; no new hardware experiments were conducted. Two-pool context-length routing (FleetOpt) delivers roughly 2.5x better tok/W over a homogeneous fleet, while upgrading from H100 to B200 delivers roughly 1.7x. The gains are independent: combining FleetOpt with B200 yields 4.25x over the H100 homogeneous baseline. B200/H200 numbers are analytical projections (+-20% uncertainty); H100 results are calibrated to published measurements.
  For MoE models, active-parameter weight streaming adds a third lever. Qwen3-235B-A22B (22B active) reaches roughly 37.8 tok/W at 8K context on H100 -- 5.1x better than Llama-3.1-70B -- because decode time scales with activated weights, not total parameters. MoE dispatch overhead is excluded, so this is an upper bound.

</details>


### [37] [ZipServ: Fast and Memory-Efficient LLM Inference with Hardware-Aware Lossless Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17435)
*Ruibo Fan,Xiangrui Yu,Xinglin Pan,Zeyu Li,Weile Luo,Qiang Wang,Wei Wang,Xiaowen Chu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: ZipServ是一个面向LLM推理的无损压缩框架，通过Tensor-Core感知的三重位图编码(TCA-TBE)和融合解压GEMM内核(ZipGEMM)，在减少模型体积的同时显著加速推理，解决了传统方法在GPU架构上的设计失配问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM无损压缩方法由于与GPU架构设计失配导致推理速度显著下降：内核层面，传统熵编解码器产生的变长比特流破坏了SIMT并行性；系统层面，解耦的流水线导致冗余的内存流量。需要设计一种与GPU架构协同优化的压缩框架来同时解决存储和带宽瓶颈。

Method: 提出Tensor-Core感知的三重位图编码(TCA-TBE)，这是一种新型定长格式，支持恒定时间并行解码；设计融合解压-GEMM内核(ZipGEMM)，在运行时直接将权重解压到Tensor Core寄存器中，消除中间缓冲区，最大化计算强度。

Result: 模型体积减少高达30%；内核级别相比NVIDIA cuBLAS加速达2.21倍；端到端推理相比vLLM平均加速1.22倍；首个同时实现存储节省和实质性加速的LLM推理无损压缩系统。

Conclusion: ZipServ证明了通过算法与硬件架构协同设计，无损压缩不仅能够节省存储空间，还能有效缓解LLM服务中的内存和带宽瓶颈，实现推理加速。这为LLM的高效部署提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Lossless model compression holds tremendous promise for alleviating the memory and bandwidth bottlenecks in bit-exact Large Language Model (LLM) serving. However, existing approaches often result in substantial inference slowdowns due to fundamental design mismatches with GPU architectures: at the kernel level, variable-length bitstreams produced by traditional entropy codecs break SIMT parallelism; at the system level, decoupled pipelines lead to redundant memory traffic. We present ZipServ, a lossless compression framework co-designed for efficient LLM inference. ZipServ introduces Tensor-Core-Aware Triple Bitmap Encoding (TCA-TBE), a novel fixed-length format that enables constant-time, parallel decoding, together with a fused decompression-GEMM (ZipGEMM) kernel that decompresses weights on-the-fly directly into Tensor Core registers. This "load-compressed, compute-decompressed" design eliminates intermediate buffers and maximizes compute intensity. Experiments show that ZipServ reduces the model size by up to 30%, achieves up to 2.21x kernel-level speedup over NVIDIA's cuBLAS, and expedites end-to-end inference by an average of 1.22x over vLLM. ZipServ is the first lossless compression system that provides both storage savings and substantial acceleration for LLM inference on GPUs.

</details>

### [38] [Entropy-Aware Task Offloading in Mobile Edge Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16949)
*Mohsen Sahraei Ardakani,Hong Wan,Rui Song*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对MEC任务卸载中的位置隐私和使用模式隐私问题，利用深度循环Q网络求解隐私增强的MDP模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有移动边缘计算（MEC）卸载研究主要关注效率，忽视了无线通信引发的用户隐私问题（使用模式与位置隐私）。

Method: 将隐私约束融入任务卸载的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）建模，并采用深度循环Q网络（DRQN）求解该优化问题。

Conclusion: 将隐私保护机制纳入MEC卸载决策过程是可行且必要的，区块链与强化学习的结合为解决此类问题提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Mobile Edge Computing (MEC) technology has been introduced to enable could computing at the edge of the network in order to help resource limited mobile devices with time sensitive data processing tasks. In this paradigm, mobile devices can offload their computationally heavy tasks to more efficient nearby MEC servers via wireless communication. Consequently, the main focus of researches on the subject has been on development of efficient offloading schemes, leaving the privacy of mobile user out. While the Blockchain technology is used as the trust mechanism for secured sharing of the data, the privacy issues induced from wireless communication, namely, usage pattern and location privacy are the centerpiece of this work. The effects of these privacy concerns on the task offloading Markov Decision Process (MDP) is addressed and the MDP is solved using a Deep Recurrent Q-Netwrok (DRQN). The Numerical simulations are presented to show the effectiveness of the proposed method.
